    <script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script>
        class ContentRotator {
            constructor(containerId) {
                this.container = document.getElementById(containerId);
                this.items = this.container.getElementsByClassName('showcase-item');
                this.navigation = document.getElementById('navPoints');
                
                this.initialize();
            }

            initialize() {
                // Create navigation points
                for (let i = 0; i < this.items.length; i++) {
                    const point = document.createElement('div');
                    point.className = 'nav-point';
                    point.addEventListener('click', () => this.showContent(i));
                    this.navigation.appendChild(point);
                }

                // Show random content on page load
                this.showRandomContent();
                
                // Add click listeners to all items
                for (let i = 0; i < this.items.length; i++) {
                    this.items[i].addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                        // Don't prevent default here so the link still works
                        // Just for logging purposes
                        console.log(`Clicked on item ${i}`);
                    });
                }
            }

            showRandomContent() {
                // Generate random index
                const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * this.items.length);
                this.showContent(randomIndex);
                console.log(`Randomly selected item ${randomIndex}`);
            }

            showContent(index) {
                // Remove current class from all items
                for (let i = 0; i < this.items.length; i++) {
                    this.items[i].classList.remove('current');
                    this.navigation.children[i].classList.remove('current');
                }
                
                // Add current class to selected item
                this.items[index].classList.add('current');
                this.navigation.children[index].classList.add('current');
            }
        }

        // Initialize the content rotator when DOM is loaded
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            const rotator = new ContentRotator('contentRotator');
        });
    </script>

			        <span class="jl_post_meta"><span class="jl_author_img_w">By<a href="https://aviationupdatesph.com/author/justin-fortalitz/" title="Posts by Justin Jaime Fortaliza" rel="author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person">Justin Jaime Fortaliza</a></span><span class="post-date">November 23, 2025</span><span class="jl_fot_share_i jl_share_l_bg jls_tooltip"><i class="jli-sharethis"></i><span class="jls_tooltip_w jls_tooltip-top"><span class="jls_tooltiptext"><span class="jls_tooltip_in"><div class="post_sw"><div class="post_s">        <div class="jl_sli_w">
        <ul class="jl_sli_in">

			        <h3 class="jl_fe_title jl_txt_2row">FedEx Boeing 767 makes emergency landing at Newark after bird strike causes engine fire</h3>
			        <span class="jl_post_meta"><span class="jl_author_img_w">By<a href="https://aviationupdatesph.com/author/dirksalcedo/" title="Posts by Dirk Andrei Salcedo" rel="author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person">Dirk Andrei Salcedo</a></span><span class="post-date">March 2, 2025</span><span class="jl_fot_share_i jl_share_l_bg jls_tooltip"><i class="jli-sharethis"></i><span class="jls_tooltip_w jls_tooltip-top"><span class="jls_tooltiptext"><span class="jls_tooltip_in"><div class="post_sw"><div class="post_s">        <div class="jl_sli_w">

			        <h3 class="jl_fe_title jl_txt_2row">Jeju Air flight crashes on landing in South Korea</h3>
			        <span class="jl_post_meta"><span class="jl_author_img_w">By<a href="https://aviationupdatesph.com/author/dirksalcedo/" title="Posts by Dirk Andrei Salcedo" rel="author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person">Dirk Andrei Salcedo</a></span><span class="post-date">December 29, 2024</span><span class="jl_fot_share_i jl_share_l_bg jls_tooltip"><i class="jli-sharethis"></i><span class="jls_tooltip_w jls_tooltip-top"><span class="jls_tooltiptext"><span class="jls_tooltip_in"><div class="post_sw"><div class="post_s">        <div class="jl_sli_w">
        <ul class="jl_sli_in">
            <li class="jl_sli_fb jl_shli"><a class="jl_sshl" href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Faviationupdatesph.com%2F2024%2F12%2Fjeju-air-flight-crashes-on-landing-in-south-korea-28-reported-dead%2F" rel="nofollow"><i class="jli-facebook"></i><span>Share</span></a></li>
